msg:A very pleasant discovery during this trip to Xi'an.
The transportation is very convenient, adjacent to Big Wild Goose Pagoda, Tang Furong Garden, and other popular check-in spots.
If you are a traveler like me who likes to stay in hotels, you can really spend a day here. The environment is elegant, comfortable and pleasant, with dense green plants and interesting construction. I found a free-range peacock at the corner, combing its feathers against the glass window and admiring its beauty.
The room is also good, and the front desk has been upgraded, which is very heartwarming.
The breakfast is a combination of Chinese and Western, with Shaanxi specialties.
The overall architecture is very traditional, the hotel lobby design is unique and unique, with a strong Tang Dynasty style. I saw the mural (Two Capitals Flower Banquet Picture) that marked the period of Sino-Japanese harmony. It is divided into four parts, each with its own theme. This painting tells us that this garden hotel was built by the cooperation of China and Japan. The two capitals refer to the ancient Chang'an and the ancient Japanese capital Yamato. Seeing this, I hope for world peace.
Priya and Lei Yuxin, the little beauty, provide good service, like it üëç
I will definitely stay here next time I go to Xi'an

After passing through the first intersection of Datang Everlasting City (there is a Starbucks on the left), follow the direction of Starbucks and walk straight to the left for 20 meters to reach the Chang'an Twelve Hours Attraction. Continue straight. You can reach the west gate of Tang Dynasty Furong Garden. There are many interesting attractions in the surrounding area that can be reached on foot, which is very convenient. msg:First of all, thanks for the upgrade of the hotel, although there was a little episode in the middle. But the hotel also quickly resolved and upgraded the room type, which is the attitude and service of a five-star hotel. Let's talk about feelings.
Facilities: Although this hotel is said to open in 2021, it is actually a bit old from the outside. Later, I learned that the prototype of the hotel was the Tanghua Hotel, which had been built for a long time and was renovated internally. So you can still see traces of the years.
Hygiene: Because it is a Chinese-style structure, there are many wooden facilities, but the wooden facilities are easy to see obvious dust, so try to clean every place on the door and table. This section is a little lacking, and the dust is still quite obvious Yes, the bathrobes may not be used by some guests, so they should not be replaced during room cleaning, and the floating dust is more obvious. The toilet recommends that the maintenance depar**ent can repair it in time, because the toilet in my room will shake, and the glass glue on the side has all cracked and fallen off, so it needs to be repaired for safety. There were some small episodes in the bed sheets. I believe the sheets were replaced because the creases were new. Maybe I didn't pay attention to the stains on the bed when I changed them. It should be a problem with the machine.
Service: The hotel's service can still meet the five-star standard. Problems are found and dealt with in a timely manner, which is very good and very good. I can't quite remember the name of that young lady, is it Karry? Good attitude and good service. The Hanfu lady at the front desk is also great. She didn't notice the brand name and gave me food to feed the peacocks. Maybe the cleaning lady needs to be strengthened. The bear was delivered to the guest room with full service from getting off the car. The service is nothing to say, üëç.
Environment: The hotel is not too big, but there is nothing to say about the environment. The free-range peacock ü¶ö is a major feature of it. Peacocks are not afraid of people, but they must not be caught. The breakfast is very rich and the taste is quite satisfactory. The amazing thing is a bottle Milk oa**eal and mutton steamed buns are also good. But there seems to be no orange juice. There is also a Black Pearl restaurant in the hotel, which may have been off work when I went.
Overall, I might consider staying at the hotel next time.
